\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_ae023cb001f3261d064f423101798d6be}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_ae023cb001f3261d064f423101798d6be}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!calculateLatencyMillis@{calculateLatencyMillis}}
\index{calculateLatencyMillis@{calculateLatencyMillis}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{calculateLatencyMillis()}{calculateLatencyMillis()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$double$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::calculate\+Latency\+Millis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Calculate the latency of a stream based on \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_acb8edbc17ff79993a8ed996d216fe6f3}{get\+Timestamp()}}.

Output latency is the time it takes for a given frame to travel from the app to some type of digital-\/to-\/analog converter. If the D\+AC is external, for example in a U\+SB interface or a TV connected by H\+D\+MI, then there may be additional latency that the Android device is unaware of.

Input latency is the time it takes to a given frame to travel from an analog-\/to-\/digital converter (A\+DC) to the app.

Note that the latency of an O\+U\+T\+P\+UT stream will increase abruptly when you write data to it and then decrease slowly over time as the data is consumed.

The latency of an I\+N\+P\+UT stream will decrease abruptly when you read data from it and then increase slowly over time as more data arrives.

The latency of an O\+U\+T\+P\+UT stream is generally higher than the I\+N\+P\+UT latency because an app generally tries to keep the O\+U\+T\+P\+UT buffer full and the I\+N\+P\+UT buffer empty.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the latency in milliseconds, or a result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Calculate the latency of a stream based on \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_acb8edbc17ff79993a8ed996d216fe6f3}{get\+Timestamp()}}.

Output latency is the time it takes for a given frame to travel from the app to some type of digital-\/to-\/analog converter. If the D\+AC is external, for example in a U\+SB interface or a TV connected by H\+D\+MI, then there may be additional latency that the Android device is unaware of.

Input latency is the time it takes to a given frame to travel from an analog-\/to-\/digital converter (A\+DC) to the app.

Note that the latency of an O\+U\+T\+P\+UT stream will increase abruptly when you write data to it and then decrease slowly over time as the data is consumed.

The latency of an I\+N\+P\+UT stream will decrease abruptly when you read data from it and then increase slowly over time as more data arrives.

The latency of an O\+U\+T\+P\+UT stream is generally higher than the I\+N\+P\+UT latency because an app generally tries to keep the O\+U\+T\+P\+UT buffer full and the I\+N\+P\+UT buffer empty.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the latency in milliseconds, or a result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Calculate the latency of a stream based on \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_acb8edbc17ff79993a8ed996d216fe6f3}{get\+Timestamp()}}.

\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!getTimestamp@{getTimestamp}}
\index{getTimestamp@{getTimestamp}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getTimestamp()}{getTimestamp()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/8]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{structoboe_1_1_frame_timestamp}{Frame\+Timestamp}}$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::get\+Timestamp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{clockid\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Get the estimated time that the frame at {\ttfamily frame\+Position} entered or left the audio processing pipeline.

This can be used to coordinate events and interactions with the external environment, and to estimate the latency of an audio stream. An example of usage can be found in the hello-\/oboe sample (search for \char`\"{}calculate\+Current\+Output\+Latency\+Millis\char`\"{}).

The time is based on the implementation\textquotesingle{}s best effort, using whatever knowledge is available to the system, but cannot account for any delay unknown to the implementation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clock\+Id} & the type of clock to use e.\+g. C\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+M\+O\+N\+O\+T\+O\+N\+IC \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{structoboe_1_1_frame_timestamp}{Frame\+Timestamp}} containing the position and time at which a particular audio frame entered or left the audio processing pipeline, or an error if the operation failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_ad1a1d3bbf3b348ed92b7ed18ce9cc261}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_ad1a1d3bbf3b348ed92b7ed18ce9cc261}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!getXRunCount@{getXRunCount}}
\index{getXRunCount@{getXRunCount}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getXRunCount()}{getXRunCount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::get\+X\+Run\+Count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

An X\+Run is an Underrun or an Overrun. During playing, an underrun will occur if the stream is not written in time and the system runs out of valid data. During recording, an overrun will occur if the stream is not read in time and there is no place to put the incoming data so it is discarded.

An underrun or overrun can cause an audible \char`\"{}pop\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}glitch\char`\"{}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a result which is either Result\+::\+OK with the x\+Run count as the value, or a Result\+::\+Error$\ast$ code 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Pause the stream. This will block until the stream has been paused, an error occurs or {\ttfamily timeout\+Nanoseconds} has been reached. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a8089f0a0cb68d4039cf33e6584129978}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a8089f0a0cb68d4039cf33e6584129978}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!read@{read}}
\index{read@{read}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{read()}{read()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Read data into the supplied buffer from the stream. This method will block until the read is complete or it runs out of time.

If {\ttfamily timeout\+Nanoseconds} is zero then this call will not wait.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em buffer} & The address of the first sample. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Frames} & Number of frames to read. Only complete frames will be read. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & Maximum number of nanoseconds to wait for completion. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the number of frames actually read, or result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Read data into the supplied buffer from the stream. This method will block until the read is complete or it runs out of time.

If {\ttfamily timeout\+Nanoseconds} is zero then this call will not wait.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em buffer} & The address of the first sample. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Frames} & Number of frames to read. Only complete frames will be read. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & Maximum number of nanoseconds to wait for completion. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the number of frames actually read, or result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a06e3f9e133b3a75515e7793939d1cd03}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a06e3f9e133b3a75515e7793939d1cd03}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!setBufferSizeInFrames@{setBufferSizeInFrames}}
\index{setBufferSizeInFrames@{setBufferSizeInFrames}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBufferSizeInFrames()}{setBufferSizeInFrames()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::set\+Buffer\+Size\+In\+Frames (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This can be used to adjust the latency of the buffer by changing the threshold where blocking will occur. By combining this with \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_ad1a1d3bbf3b348ed92b7ed18ce9cc261}{get\+X\+Run\+Count()}}, the latency can be tuned at run-\/time for each device.

This cannot be set higher than get\+Buffer\+Capacity().


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em requested\+Frames} & requested number of frames that can be filled without blocking \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the resulting buffer size in frames (obtained using value()) or an error (obtained using error()) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!waitForAvailableFrames@{waitForAvailableFrames}}
\index{waitForAvailableFrames@{waitForAvailableFrames}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{waitForAvailableFrames()}{waitForAvailableFrames()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::wait\+For\+Available\+Frames (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{num\+Frames,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+Nanoseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Wait until the stream has a minimum amount of data available in its buffer. This can be used with an E\+X\+C\+L\+U\+S\+I\+VE M\+M\+AP input stream to avoid reading data too close to the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_d_s_p}{D\+SP}} write position, which may cause glitches.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em num\+Frames} & minimum frames available \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
number of frames available, Error\+Timeout 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a8816ebd1445282469fb7e27899263deb}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a8816ebd1445282469fb7e27899263deb}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::wait\+For\+Available\+Frames (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{num\+Frames,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+Nanoseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a0c865a5501f369d959c39d8ab8b46a07}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a0c865a5501f369d959c39d8ab8b46a07}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!waitForStateChange@{waitForStateChange}}
\index{waitForStateChange@{waitForStateChange}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{waitForStateChange()}{waitForStateChange()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a486512e787b609c80ba4436f23929af1}{Result}} oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::wait\+For\+State\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}}}]{input\+State,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}} $\ast$}]{next\+State,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+Nanoseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Wait until the stream\textquotesingle{}s current state no longer matches the input state. The input state is passed to avoid race conditions caused by the state changing between calls.

Note that generally applications do not need to call this. It is considered an advanced technique and is mostly used for testing.


\begin{DoxyPre}{\ttfamily 
int64\_t timeoutNanos = 500 * kNanosPerMillisecond; // arbitrary 1/2 second
StreamState currentState = stream-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a9d37cc6513823c685ae892626ff83ea8}{getState()}};
StreamState nextState = StreamState::Unknown;
while (result == Result::OK \&\& currentState != StreamState::Paused) \{
    result = stream-\/>waitForStateChange(
                                  currentState, \&nextState, timeoutNanos);
    currentState = nextState;
\}
}\end{DoxyPre}


If the state does not change within the timeout period then it will return Error\+Timeout. This is true even if timeout\+Nanoseconds is zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em input\+State} & The state we want to change away from. \\
\hline
{\em next\+State} & Pointer to a variable that will be set to the new state. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & The maximum time to wait in nanoseconds. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Result\+::\+OK or a Result\+::\+Error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Implemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_filter_audio_stream_a0f5477e0eeb250513a222d1a51114fc8}{oboe\+::\+Filter\+Audio\+Stream}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_filter_audio_stream_a0f5477e0eeb250513a222d1a51114fc8}{oboe\+::\+Filter\+Audio\+Stream}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_filter_audio_stream_a0f5477e0eeb250513a222d1a51114fc8}{oboe\+::\+Filter\+Audio\+Stream}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_filter_audio_stream_a0f5477e0eeb250513a222d1a51114fc8}{oboe\+::\+Filter\+Audio\+Stream}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_open_s_l_e_s_a16da90f5ea20b0ead2d3ff5c7f54586a}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+Open\+S\+L\+ES}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_open_s_l_e_s_ac46eea0936b4ffed37c29d1bda9645eb}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+Open\+S\+L\+ES}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_open_s_l_e_s_ac46eea0936b4ffed37c29d1bda9645eb}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+Open\+S\+L\+ES}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_open_s_l_e_s_ac46eea0936b4ffed37c29d1bda9645eb}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+Open\+S\+L\+ES}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a_audio_a4a34fe906f8090630a40028e2db2c6b2}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+A\+Audio}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a_audio_a4a34fe906f8090630a40028e2db2c6b2}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+A\+Audio}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a_audio_a4a34fe906f8090630a40028e2db2c6b2}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+A\+Audio}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a_audio_a4a34fe906f8090630a40028e2db2c6b2}{oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+A\+Audio}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a486512e787b609c80ba4436f23929af1}{Result}} oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::wait\+For\+State\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}}}]{input\+State,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}} $\ast$}]{next\+State,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+Nanoseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Wait until the stream\textquotesingle{}s current state no longer matches the input state. The input state is passed to avoid race conditions caused by the state changing between calls.

Note that generally applications do not need to call this. It is considered an advanced technique and is mostly used for testing.


\begin{DoxyPre}{\ttfamily 
int64\_t timeoutNanos = 500 * kNanosPerMillisecond; // arbitrary 1/2 second
StreamState currentState = stream-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a9d37cc6513823c685ae892626ff83ea8}{getState()}};
StreamState nextState = StreamState::Unknown;
while (result == Result::OK \&\& currentState != StreamState::Paused) \{
    result = stream-\/>waitForStateChange(
                                  currentState, \&nextState, timeoutNanos);
    currentState = nextState;
\}
}\end{DoxyPre}


If the state does not change within the timeout period then it will return Error\+Timeout. This is true even if timeout\+Nanoseconds is zero.

\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a0c865a5501f369d959c39d8ab8b46a07}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a0c865a5501f369d959c39d8ab8b46a07}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!waitForStateChange@{waitForStateChange}}
\index{waitForStateChange@{waitForStateChange}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{waitForStateChange()}{waitForStateChange()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a486512e787b609c80ba4436f23929af1}{Result}} oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::wait\+For\+State\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}}}]{input\+State,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoboe_a89fa2ce046723764618c29db737917f6}{Stream\+State}} $\ast$}]{next\+State,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+Nanoseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Wait until the stream\textquotesingle{}s current state no longer matches the input state. The input state is passed to avoid race conditions caused by the state changing between calls.

Note that generally applications do not need to call this. It is considered an advanced technique and is mostly used for testing.


\begin{DoxyPre}{\ttfamily 
int64\_t timeoutNanos = 500 * kNanosPerMillisecond; // arbitrary 1/2 second
StreamState currentState = stream-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a9d37cc6513823c685ae892626ff83ea8}{getState()}};
StreamState nextState = StreamState::Unknown;
while (result == Result::OK \&\& currentState != StreamState::Paused) \{
    result = stream-\/>waitForStateChange(
                                  currentState, \&nextState, timeoutNanos);
    currentState = nextState;
\}
}\end{DoxyPre}


If the state does not change within the timeout period then it will return Error\+Timeout. This is true even if timeout\+Nanoseconds is zero.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em input\+State} & The state we want to change away from. \\
\hline
{\em next\+State} & Pointer to a variable that will be set to the new state. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & The maximum time to wait in nanoseconds. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Result\+::\+OK or a Result\+::\+Error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

This is used to detect more than one error callback from a stream. These were bugs in some versions of Android that caused multiple error callbacks. Internal bug b/63087953

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a3612c05ed6b01a213dde67d913c07e11}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a3612c05ed6b01a213dde67d913c07e11}} 
\index{oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}!write@{write}}
\index{write@{write}!oboe::AudioStream@{oboe::AudioStream}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{write()}{write()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Write data from the supplied buffer into the stream. This method will block until the write is complete or it runs out of time.

If {\ttfamily timeout\+Nanoseconds} is zero then this call will not wait.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em buffer} & The address of the first sample. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Frames} & Number of frames to write. Only complete frames will be written. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & Maximum number of nanoseconds to wait for completion. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the number of frames actually written, or result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{write()}{write()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}}$<$int32\+\_\+t$>$ oboe\+::\+Audio\+Stream\+::write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{int32\+\_\+t}]{,  }\item[{int64\+\_\+t}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Write data from the supplied buffer into the stream. This method will block until the write is complete or it runs out of time.

If {\ttfamily timeout\+Nanoseconds} is zero then this call will not wait.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em buffer} & The address of the first sample. \\
\hline
{\em num\+Frames} & Number of frames to write. Only complete frames will be written. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Nanoseconds} & Maximum number of nanoseconds to wait for completion. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a \mbox{\hyperlink{classoboe_1_1_result_with_value}{Result\+With\+Value}} which has a result of Result\+::\+OK and a value containing the number of frames actually written, or result of Result\+::\+Error$\ast$. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mFramesRead}{mFramesRead}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::atomic$<$ int64\+\_\+t $>$ Audio\+Stream\+::m\+Frames\+Read \{\}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Number of frames which have been read from the stream.

This is signed integer to match the counters in A\+Audio. At audio rates, the counter will overflow in about six million years. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a9ac61e75894badbc2513977e89ef8a9b}\label{classoboe_1_1_audio_stream_a9ac61e75894badbc2513977e89ef8a9b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::atomic$<$ int64\+\_\+t $>$ Audio\+Stream\+::m\+Frames\+Written \{\}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Number of frames which have been written into the stream

This is signed integer to match the counters in A\+Audio. At audio rates, the counter will overflow in about six million years.
